### 1. E-Girl 黄金时段光线下的镜面自拍（重复）

**Author**: [Sudee🥀](https://x.com/NameIsSudee)  **Date**: 2026-01-19  **Language**: en

> 一个详细的 JSON 提示，用于 Gemini Nano Banana Pro，专注于生成一张具有“e-girl”或“软颓废”美学风格的女性逼真镜面自拍。它指定了铂金色头发、带有卡通印花的白色缎面紧身胸衣，以及沐浴在温暖金色夕阳下的室内走廊环境。（重复 2013095567547666866）

![E-Girl 黄金时段光线下的镜面自拍（重复）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768890709718_8jx82s_G-_pBv0W0AAv4gM.jpg)

```
{
  "prompt_description": {
    "subject": {
      "type": "woman",
      "hair": "long, straight, platinum blonde",
      "features": "light skin tone, soft makeup, finger resting on lip",
      "tattoos": "small text tattoo on chest, 'XXX' tattoo on wrist"
    },
    "outfit": {
      "top": "white satin corset with pink cartoon/anime print ({argument name="cartoon character" default="My Melody"} style), lace trim, ribbon tie front",
      "bottom": "black pleated mini skirt, raw hem",
      "accessories": "black lace-top thigh-high stockings, fishnet tights",
      "phone_case": "graphic black and white anime style illustration"
    },
    "pose": {
      "type": "mirror selfie",
      "stance": "standing, one hip popped",
      "hand_position": "holding phone with right hand, left hand touching lip"
    },
    "environment": {
      "location": "indoor hallway or bedroom",
      "background": "white walls, grey tiled floor, framed posters on wall",
      "lighting": "warm golden hour sunlight, soft shadows",
      "decor": "minimalist, potted plant in background"
    },
    "style": {
      "aesthetic": "e-girl, soft grunge, coquette, trendy",
      "camera_angle": "eye level, reflection",
      "quality": "high definition, photorealistic, vivid colors"
    }
  }
}

### 2. 带猫耳和格子裙的镜面自拍提示词

**Author**: [sammy](https://x.com/sumiturkude007)  **Date**: 2026-01-18  **Language**: en

> 一个结构化的 JSON 提示词，用于生成一张年轻女性的镜面自拍照，她身穿俏皮的粉色主题服装（猫耳朵、锦缎紧身胸衣、格子裙）。提示词指定了姿势（吐舌头）、背景（带城市景观的现代公寓），并包含文本叠加“HIII”。

![带猫耳和格子裙的镜面自拍提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768804222907_g8op6a_G-99kVrXoAAnoal.jpg)

```
{
  "prompt": {
    "subject": {
      "description": "A young woman with long blonde hair and fair skin, wearing white fluffy cat ears headband.",
      "attire": {
        "top": "Pink brocade corset with front lacing and trim.",
        "bottom": "Pink gingham ruffled mini skirt with white lace trim.",
        "accessories": "Pink collar choker with a small silver bell, white thigh socks with pink stripes at the top.",
        "jewelry": "Small stud earrings, delicate gold bracelet."
      },
      "expression": "Playful, looking up and to the left with tongue sticking out, slight smile, light eye makeup with winged liner, pink lip color, rosy cheeks, defined nose.",
      "action": "Taking a mirror selfie with a white iPhone held in her right hand, showing her reflection."
    },
    "background": {
      "setting": "Modern apartment interior.",
      "elements": "Large floor-to-ceiling windows showing a bright daytime cityscape and sky.",
      "flooring": "Grey wood plank flooring.",
      "objects": {
        "left_side": "Large brown teddy bear leaning against a grey tiled wall section.",
        "right_side": "White upholstered armchair, wooden side table, green artificial ivy plant hanging in the foreground, clear glass vase on a shelf.",
        "reflection": "The mirror itself shows the reflection of the subject and the room.",
        "text": "White text '{argument name=\"text overlay\" default=\"HIII\"}' overlaying the background near the chair."
      },
      "lighting": "Bright natural daylight from the windows."
    },
    "style": "Mirror selfie photograph.",

### 3. Z 世代网红在柔和色调走廊里的镜面自拍

**Author**: [KeorUnreal](https://x.com/KeorUnreal)  **Date**: 2026-01-18  **Language**: en

> 一个高度详细、逼真的图像生成提示，用于制作一张具有 Z 世代网红美学的镜面自拍。它详细描述了拍摄对象的形象（铂金色太空发髻、特定妆容）、服装（柔和的绿色褶皱抹胸连衣裙、橙色高跟鞋）、姿势（跪姿、拉扯头发），以及一个详细的柔和色调的家庭走廊环境，包括具体的手机细节。

![Z 世代网红在柔和色调走廊里的镜面自拍](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768804290245_yyhrbj_G-8HddUX0AAJbA4.jpg)
![Z 世代网红在柔和色调走廊里的镜面自拍](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768804290325_vsx8to_G-8w2MhWsAANB8i.jpg)
![Z 世代网红在柔和色调走廊里的镜面自拍](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768804290419_4oztcw_G-8w2OvWIAAvfYU.jpg)

```
{

    "prompt_version": "2.0",
    "use_case": "Photorealistic Image Generation",
    "main_subject_count": 1
  },
  "subject_layer": {

        "gender": "Female",

      },

          "color": "Blue",
          "makeup": "Sharp black winged eyeliner, defined lashes"
        },

          "lip_color": "Soft pink, natural"
        },
        "complexion_accents": "Heavy rosy pink blush across cheeks and nose bridge (sun-kissed look)"
      },
      "hair": {
        "color": "Platinum blonde",
        "style_core": "Two messy high space buns",
        "framing": "Long loose tendrils framing the face",
        "interaction": "Subject is pulling one long strand sideways with left hand"
      }
    },
    "attire_layer": {
      "garment_main": {
        "item": "Tube dress",
        "length": "Mini",
        "fit": "Tight/Bodycon",
        "color": "{argument name="dress color" default="Pastel green lime"}",
        "texture": "Ruched fabric, natural horizontal folds"
      },
      "accessories": {
        "neck": "Chunky turquoise/teal beaded choker"
      },
      "footwear": {
        "type": "High heels stiletto",
        "visibility": "One shoe visible on raised foot",
        "color_way": "Orange"
      }
    },
    "pose_dynamics": {

        "right_arm": "Raised holding phone near face",

### 7. Y2K 浴室镜自拍提示词（图生图）

**Author**: [Sharon Riley](https://x.com/Just_sharon7)  **Date**: 2026-01-18  **Language**: en

> 一个结构化的 JSON 提示词，用于生成一张逼真、随意的性感浴室镜子自拍，要求使用参考图像来确定拍摄对象的面部。它详细描述了 Y2K 风格的服装（低腰牛仔裤、带文字的露脐 T 恤、可见的微型丁字裤）以及小纹身等配饰。

![Y2K 浴室镜自拍提示词（图生图）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768804217512_727qtn_G-7gguQWEAAmf21.jpg)

```
{
  "subject": {
    "age": 20,
    "gender": "female",
    "ethnicity": "western",
    "appearance": {
      "face": "same as reference image, do not change facial features",
      "features": "delicate",
      "eyes": "big, expressive",
      "makeup": "natural",
      "expression": "slight pout, looking at camera",
      "hair": {
        "color": "blonde",
        "style": "messy high voluminous bun",
        "texture": "wavy"
      }
    }
  },
  "clothing": {
    "top": {
      "type": "cropped baby-t-shirt",
      "color": "dark brown",
      "text": "{argument name=\"shirt text\" default=\"EVERYTHING'S BIGGER IN TEXAS\"}",
      "fit": "tight"
    },
    "bottom": {
      "type": "jeans",
      "color": "blue",
      "style": "very low rise, loose"
    },
    "underwear": {
      "type": "micro thong",
      "color": "bright pink",
      "visibility": "visible high on hips"
    }
  },
  "accessories": {
    "tattoos": [
      {"location": "hand", "design": "small star"},
      {"location": "lower stomach", "design": "small heart"}
    ],
    "nails": "colorful butterfly"
  },
  "pose": "bathroom mirror selfie",
  "lighting": "warm indoor",
  "vibe": "casual sexy",
  "style": "realistic, photorealistic",
  "details": {
    "skin": "detailed texture",
    "resolution": "8k"

}

### 8. 镜中自拍内衣姿势提示，带透视缩短效果

**Author**: [Mikasa](https://x.com/Mikasa_rose729)  **Date**: 2026-01-18  **Language**: en

> 一个高度具体的 JSON 提示，用于生成一张女性在现代酒店房间内，身穿黑色内衣的镜面自拍照。该提示详细说明了姿势，包括左腿的极端透视缩短、特定的手势，并要求物理上正确的反射以及使用上传的参考图像来识别身份。

        "expression": "neutral, confident, slightly relaxed"
      },
      "accessories": [
        {
          "type": "headwear",
          "style": "beige cable-knit beret, slightly tilted"

          "type": "necklace",
          "style": "thin, delicate gold necklace"
        },

Subject: A cute 19-year-old Caucasian girl with a youthful, fresh face and long, messy-wavy blonde/light-brown hair.* 

Physique: She has a fit, curvy body with a slim waist and wider hips.*   

Pose: She stands in front of a tall floor mirror. She adopts a flattering pose: one leg is stepped slightly forward, and she pops her hip to the side, accentuating her curves. 

She holds an iPhone (with a cute case) up to the mirror. She is looking at the phone screen in the reflection, not the camera.

Outfit (The "Lazy-Hot" Look):*   

Top: A tight, white ribbed tank top or baby tee, cropped short to show her midriff and belly button.*   

Bottom: Grey sweatpants worn low-rise (rolled down at the waist) to highlight her waist-to-hip ratio.

Environment: The room is a typical teenager's bedroom. Unmade bed in the background, soft LED strip lights (purple or warm white) on the ceiling, and maybe some clothes on a chair. It feels lived-in and authentic.

Lighting: Natural light coming from a window mixed with the soft indoor room light, creating a flattering, soft glow on her skin.

> 一个详细的 JSON 提示，用于生成一张年轻女性在室内优雅蹲姿的 8K 镜面自拍。它要求严格保留参考图像中的面部，并指定了服装（黑色皮质超短裙、及踝靴）、姿势和环境（裸露的砖墙、温暖柔和的灯光），以营造出优雅的社交媒体美学。

    "face_preservation": {
      "use_reference_face": true,
      "accuracy": "match face exactly from reference image",
      "preserve_details": [
        "face shape",
        "eyebrows and eye structure",
        "natural makeup style",
        "lip shape and color",
        "hairline and hairstyle"
      ]
    },

        "body_position": "squatting low with one knee forward, leaning slightly toward mirror",
        "head": "tilted slightly downward while looking at phone screen",
        "hands": [
          "right hand holding phone in front of face",
          "left hand resting on knee"
        ],
        "expression": "soft, calm expression"
      },
      "hair": {
        "style": "long dark brown hair in a half-up ponytail with a small clip",
        "texture": "smooth and straight"
      },
      "attire": {
        "dress": {
          "type": "black leather micro-skirt with fitted top",
          "pattern": "plain with metallic accents",
          "details": "slit exposing leg, edgy structured flow"
        },
        "shoes": "black ankle boots",
        "accessories": [
          "choker necklace",
          "stud earrings",
          "leather bracelet"
        ]
      }
    },
    "environment": {
      "setting": "indoor room with soft lighting",
      "background": "exposed brick wall with urban art posters",
      "floor": "smooth, reflective surface",
      "lighting": {
        "type": "soft warm indoor light",
        "effect": "even illumination on face and dress"
      }
    },
    "props": {
      "phone": {
        "type": "smartphone",
        "case": "glitter silver phone case",
        "position": "held vertically towards the mirror"
      }
    },
    "style": {
      "photography": "mirror selfie, social media aesthetic",

      "mood": "feminine, elegant, gentle"
    },

### 73. 保留面部细节的全身镜面自拍图像生成

**Author**: [𝐌𝐢𝐧𝐝𝐒𝐩𝐚𝐫𝐤](https://x.com/Strength04_X)  **Date**: 2025-12-11  **Language**: en

> 一个用于生成 8K 超逼真镜面自拍的复杂 JSON 提示。它要求精确保留参考图像中的面部，并详细说明了拍摄对象的姿势（低蹲）、服装（黑色罗纹紧身迷你连衣裙、高跟鞋）和环境（带暖色照明的现代房间）。它还包含特定的负面提示，以确保高质量。

        "body_position": "low squat with heel slightly lifted, leaning in confidently",
        "head": "slightly tilted, gaze downward at phone",

      },

      },

### 74. 电梯随拍镜面自拍

**Author**: [𝗦𝗮𝗻𝗶𝗮](https://x.com/saniaspeaks_)  **Date**: 2025-12-11  **Language**: en

> 一个为 Nano Banana Pro 设计的详细双结构提示，用于生成一张在现代电梯内拍摄的逼真、随意的镜子自拍照。它详细说明了主体（长棕发年轻女性，生动的笑容）、服装（黑色上衣）、环境（拉丝不锈钢、LED 照明）和美学（电影感、高分辨率、自发社交媒体快照风格）。

![电梯随拍镜面自拍](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765967680207_pe38h5_G74bOltaIAAWLWk.jpg)

```
{
  "image_prompt": {
    "subject": {
      "description": "Young woman with long, layered brown hair.",
      "outfit": "Black long-sleeved top or blazer.",
      "expression": "Genuine, animated smile with mouth slightly open as if mid-sentence or laughing. Eyes looking towards the phone screen/reflection."
    },
    "pose_and_action": {
      "type": "Mirror selfie.",
      "details": "Standing pose, holding a smartphone aloft in one hand to capture reflection. Opposite hand resting casually on hip. Head tilted slightly in a relaxed manner."
    },
    "environment": {
      "location": "Modern elevator interior.",
      "elements": "Brushed stainless steel walls and doors, subtle wood paneling accents, elevator button panel with illuminated buttons.",
      "reflections": "Glossy metallic surfaces reflecting the subject and the depth of the confined space."
    },
    "lighting": {
      "source": "Soft, even overhead LED strip lighting.",
      "quality": "Flattering, diffuse light with subtle highlights on hair and skin. Cool tones from the metal contrasting with warm skin tones."
    },
    "technical_style": {
      "aesthetic": "Photorealistic, candid, cinematic, high resolution, 8k.",
      "vibe": "Spontaneous, intimate, social media snapshot style."
    }
  },
  "full_combined_prompt": "A photorealistic mirror selfie of a young woman with long brown hair inside a modern elevator. She is wearing a black outfit, holding a smartphone to take the photo, and resting one hand on her hip. She has a genuine, animated smile with her mouth slightly open as if speaking. The background features brushed stainless steel panels, metal doors, and elevator buttons. The lighting is soft and overhead, creating reflections on the metallic surfaces. The vibe is candid and spontaneous. High detail, 8k resolution."
}
```

> 一个高度具体的 JSON 提示，用于生成女性对象的超现实、全身镜面或自拍式肖像。它要求严格保留参考图像中的面部特征、发型和腹部纹身，并详细说明了服装、极简背景以及特定的智能手机相机设置，以呈现高质量、自信的美感。

    },
    "expression": "serious and confident",

      "right_hand": "holding a cell phone taking the photo",
      "left_hand": "playing with hair",
      "stance": "standing against a wall, facing the camera"
    },
    "appearance": {
      "hair": {
        "color": "dark",
        "length": "long",
        "style": "straight bangs with two long thick braids over the shoulders"
      },
      "makeup": {
        "style": "dramatic",
        "details": [
          "winged eyeliner",
          "lipstick"
        ]
      },
      "tattoos": {
        "location": "abdomen",
        "visibility": "discreet but visible"
      }
    }
  },
  "wardrobe": {
    "top": "black cropped top with red inverted text reading \"I'M F***ING STAR\"",
    "bottoms": "short, tight denim shorts",
    "accessories": [
      "necklace with heart pendant"
    ]
  },
  "scene": {

      "color": "dark or black",
      "style": "simple, minimalist"
    }
  },

    "type": "soft, diffuse frontal lighting",
    "contrast": "low",
    "shadows": "minimal, no harsh shadows"

**Author**: [Melisa♡](https://x.com/xmliisu)  **Date**: 2025-12-10  **Language**: en

{
  "generation_settings": {
    "aspect_ratio": "9:16",
    "style": "Photorealistic Portrait",
    "reference_strength": "High (Face Consistency)"
  },
  "prompt_components": {
    "subject": {
      "face_reference": "Identical face to uploaded image",
      "hair": "Long, silver-grey, sleek, straight",
      "skin": "Naturally smooth with a subtle glow",
      "makeup": "Polished and naturally glamorous, winged eyeliner, defined brows, soft contouring, matte nude lips",
      "nails": "Long, painted pastel pink"
    },
    "attire": {
      "top": "Fitted white short-sleeved crop top",
      "bottoms": "Light blue high-waisted denim jeans"
    },
    "pose_and_action": {
      "type": "Mirror selfie",
      "device": "iPhone 16 Pro Max held in one hand",
      "posture": "Standing slightly turned to the side, upper body angled toward mirror, head turned toward camera, arm resting naturally by side",
      "effect": "Soft, natural side profile emphasizing waist and hips"
    },
    "environment": {
      "location": "Bright, softly lit bedroom",
      "background_elements": "Neatly made white bed with a pale pink blanket, minimalist decor",
      "lighting_source": "Soft daylight coming through windows"
    },
    "technical_details": {
      "lighting_quality": "Even and diffuse, enhancing realistic skin texture and denim details",
      "resolution": "Ultra-sharp, high-quality photorealistic 8K rendering",
      "reflection": "Clean mirror reflection"
    }
  },
  "final_prompt_string": "A realistic mirror selfie portrait of a young woman with a face identical to the reference image. She has long, sleek, straight silver-grey hair and polished makeup with winged eyeliner and matte nude lips. She is dressed in a fitted white short-sleeved crop top and light blue high-waisted denim jeans. She stands in a side profile pose, angling her body toward the mirror while holding an iPhone 16 Pro Max; her nails are long and pastel pink. The background is a sunlit bedroom with a white bed and pale pink blanket. The lighting is diffuse and soft, highlighting skin texture. 8K resolution, photorealistic."
}

### 77. 详细的镜面自拍/室内肖像提示

**Author**: [آیت شاہ](https://x.com/kashmir_ki_lark)  **Date**: 2025-12-10  **Language**: en

> 一个高度结构化的 JSON 格式提示，用于 Google Gemini Nano Banana Pro 3.0，详细描述了如何创建一张精致的镜面自拍/室内肖像。它细致地描述了拍摄对象的样貌、服装、场景（包括砖墙和柜台物品等背景元素）、灯光、构图以及所需的审美效果。

![详细的镜面自拍/室内肖像提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765509756717_dbg38y_G70d3wFaMAMLCki.jpg)

```
{
  "prompt_details": {
    "image_type": "Mirror Selfie/Indoor Portrait",
    "subject": {
      "description": "A young woman, likely in her 20s or early 30s, with fair skin and shoulder-length blonde or light brown hair.",
      "pose": "Holding a black smartphone with both hands to take a mirror selfie, looking directly into the camera/mirror with a soft expression.",
      "attire": "Wearing a silky, long-sleeved, collared white or cream-colored blouse/shirt. The bottom is a high-waisted, reddish-brown or rust-colored leather or faux-leather skirt or trousers, cinched with a matching belt. She is wearing small hoop earrings and a ring.",
      "makeup": "A deep berry or mauve lip color, and natural eye makeup."
    },
    "setting": {
      "location_type": "Bathroom or dressing area",
      "background_elements": "A prominent, large, black-framed mirror with a curved top and slightly distressed surface. Below the mirror is a narrow white ledge/counter. Behind the counter, there's exposed reddish-orange brick and a white wainscoting/beadboard below the mirror. To the right, a white electrical outlet with visible switches. To the left, a light gray towel or garment hangs on a hook/bar.",
      "lighting": "Soft, warm, indoor lighting, likely natural light supplemented by overhead fixtures, casting a subtle shine on the white blouse."
    },
    "foreground_elements": {
      "objects_on_counter": "Various makeup and beauty products are neatly arranged on the white counter directly below the mirror. These include: a bright yellow box with black text (possibly 'GOODWOLF' or similar), black and silver mascara/applicator tubes, several lip pencils (red/brown tones), a silver egg-shaped object, a white cylinder tube, various makeup brushes, and a pinkish cream stick product.",
      "focus": "Sharp focus on the subject and the reflection in the mirror."
    },
    "style_and_aesthetics": {
      "mood": "Candid, sophisticated, getting ready, natural.",
      "color_palette": "Dominantly neutral tones (white, gray) contrasted with warm accents (red brick, rust pants, berry lips) and the black mirror frame.",
      "composition": "The subject is centered in the frame, captured via the mirror reflection. The composition includes a significant portion of the surroundings, following the rule of thirds with the subject's face slightly above center."
    },
    "camera_settings": {
      "shot_type": "Close-up/Medium Shot (as seen in the mirror)",
      "perspective": "First-person (from the phone's perspective, reflecting the taker)",
      "depth_of_field": "Shallow to medium, isolating the woman and the immediate foreground products from the deeper background elements like the brick."
    }
  }
}
```

### 79. 柔和私密镜中自拍（基于参考图生成）

**Author**: [Melisa♡](https://x.com/xmliisu)  **Date**: 2025-12-10  **Language**: en

> 一个极其详细的 Gemini Nano Banana Pro JSON 提示词，专注于生成一张逼真的、私密的镜面自拍。至关重要的是，它使用 controlnet 设置和严格的身份锁定，以确保生成的图像在面部特征、皮肤纹理和整体外观上 100% 符合上传的参考图像，同时描述了场景和服装（米色针织毛衣，金色项链）。

![柔和私密镜中自拍（基于参考图生成）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765509776538_hw1noz_G7zoMkLWIAAoM_M.jpg)

```
{
  "task": "image_generation",
  "metadata": {
    "title": "Soft Intimate Mirror Selfie",
    "style": "Photorealistic, Candid, Minimalist",
    "subject": "Young Woman"
  },
  "parameters": {
    "width": 1200,
    "height": 1200,
    "aspect_ratio": "1:1",
    "format": "png"
  },
  "prompts": {
    "positive": "A soft, intimate mirror selfie of a young woman, taking complete reference from the uploaded image for her exact face, expression, hairstyle, and natural skin texture. Preserve her real features, warm complexion, natural glow, visible pores, subtle contouring, defined brows, and soft matte lips exactly as in the reference. She stands indoors in a cozy, feminine room with muted pink walls, rattan storage baskets, and soft curtains in the background. The overall atmosphere is warm, calm, and inviting. Her shoulder-length hair is styled in natural, wet-textured waves that frame her face beautifully. She is wearing an off-shoulder, cream-colored knitted sweater with a loose, relaxed fit that drapes smoothly across her collarbones. A delicate gold necklace with a heart-shaped pendant rests at the center of her chest. Her pose is soft and effortless—one hand adjusting her hair while the other holds a pale pink phone with a minimal matte case. In her arm, she carries a small white quilted designer handbag with gold hardware, heart stitching, and a structured silhouette. Lighting should match the reference: soft, diffused daylight that highlights her skin naturally without smoothing or artificial retouching. Capture true fabric texture, hair strands, skin details, and all realistic shadows. The mood is feminine, gentle, candid, and aesthetically minimal—like a warm, everyday beauty moment captured effortlessly.",
    "negative": "low quality, blurry, airbrushed, plastic skin, artificial smoothing, cartoon, illustration, 3d render, distorted hands, bad anatomy, harsh contrast, dark shadows, neon colors, clutter, messy background, watermark, text"
  },
  "reference_settings": {
    "use_controlnet": true,
    "control_mode": "face_structure_and_skin",
    "strength": 1.0,
    "note": "Ensure strict adherence to uploaded reference image for facial features and skin texture."
  }
}
```

### 80. 详细的镜面自拍生成提示

**Author**: [Lex](https://x.com/lexx_aura)  **Date**: 2025-12-10  **Language**: en

> 一个为 Gemini 上的 Nano Banana Pro 设计的高度结构化 JSON 提示，详细描述了镜子自拍图像的各个方面。它指定了拍摄对象的人口统计信息、服装（粉色毛绒猫耳、北欧毛衣）、姿势（顽皮的“嘶嘶”表情、镜子自拍）、环境（带小彩灯的宿舍房间）以及技术相机设置（24mm 镜头、柯达 Portra 400 模拟、8k 分辨率）。

      "color_grading": "Soft pastel palette, low contrast, desaturated shadows, warm cozy tones",

    }

### 81. Instagram 审美镜面自拍，搭配龙纹手机壳

**Author**: [Sharon Riley](https://x.com/Just_sharon7)  **Date**: 2025-12-09  **Language**: en

### 82. 详细的社交媒体镜面自拍肖像

**Author**: [Lex](https://x.com/lexx_aura)  **Date**: 2025-12-09  **Language**: en

> 一个极其详细、结构化的 JSON 提示，用于生成一张超逼真的社交媒体镜面自拍。它详细说明了拍摄对象的年龄、性别、发型、妆容、纹身、服装（包括特定的珠宝和手机壳等科技配饰）、凌乱的梳妆台环境，以及技术性的灯光细节，以模仿网红室内弱光手机照片的美学效果。

![详细的社交媒体镜面自拍肖像](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765440089857_5ma6qh_G7t1I7xbIAAZ65i.jpg)

```
{
  "prompt_configuration": {
    "type": "photorealistic",
    "style": "social_media_mirror_selfie",
    "viewpoint": "eye_level_reflection"
  },
  "subject_details": {
    "demographics": "Young adult female, light skin tone, slender build",
    "hair": {
      "color": "Dark brown/black",
      "style": "Long, straight, layered",
      "action": "Left hand raised, fingers running through hair on the left side, lifting it slightly away from the face"
    },
    "face": {
      "expression": "Calm, confident, soft smile, eyes looking at phone screen in reflection",
      "makeup": {
        "eyes": "Sharp black winged eyeliner, defined lashes",
        "brows": "Sculpted and defined arches",
        "lips": "Natural pink tone, soft matte finish"
      },
      "piercings": "Small silver stud in right nostril"
    },
    "body_art": {
      "left_arm": "Full sleeve tattoo featuring botanical elements, leaves, and floral shading in black and grey ink",
      "right_forearm": "Stylized fine-line illustration of a woman's face/portrait",
      "torso": "Minimalist fine-line tattoo of a face located centrally on the upper stomach/ribcage"
    }
  },
  "attire_and_accessories": {
    "clothing": {
      "top": "White cropped tank top, ribbed cotton texture, high neck, racerback cut",
      "bottom": "Dark athletic pants or sweatpants with white vertical stripes on the waistband",
      "fit": "Form-fitting, revealing midriff"
    },
    "jewelry": {
      "necklaces": [
        "Gold chain with a small circular pendant (shorter length)",
        "Gold chain with a heart-shaped pendant (longer length)"
      ]
    },
    "tech": {
      "device": "iPhone Pro model",
      "case": "Holographic purple/blue iridescent case with wavy/psychedelic liquid pattern",
      "held_by": "Right hand, fingers gripping the bottom and side"
    }
  },
  "environment_and_clutter": {
    "setting": "Personal vanity area/bedroom",
    "foreground_objects_on_counter": {
      "left": "Large yellow cylindrical tub (hair mask or cream)",
      "center": "Beige matte rectangular hair claw clip",
      "bottom_center": "Pink plastic organizer tray filled with multiple pairs of false eyelashes",
      "right": "Stack of makeup compacts and a white bottle with red cap"
    },
    "background_reflection": {
      "wall_decor": "Framed square print featuring bird silhouettes on a branch and text reading 'BE YOUR SELF' (text is reversed in mirror)",
      "hanging_items": "Blue electrical cord for a hair tool hanging on the left side"
    },
    "mirror_frame": "Vanity mirror with large exposed round bulbs visible on the left and right edges"
    
  },
  "lighting_and_atmosphere": {
    "lighting_source": "Vanity bulbs creating a bright, frontal illumination",
    "contrast": "Soft shadows, highlighted face and chest",
    "visual_quality": "Slightly hazy/grainy texture typical of indoor low-light phone photography",
    "color_palette": "Muted neutral"
  }
}

> 一个高度结构化的 JSON 提示，旨在生成一张在金属电梯内拍摄的粗犷、现代街头服饰风格的智能手机镜面自拍。它包含图像风格、主体姿势、服装、配饰、环境的详细参数，并明确要求与参考图像进行 100% 的面部身份匹配。

```
{
      "image_parameters": {
        "style": "Smartphone mirror selfie",

        "quality": "Sharp digital noise, slightly desaturated",
        "tone": "Cool, edgy, modern, industrial",
        "lighting_and_atmosphere": "Overhead fluorescent elevator lighting, unflattering but gritty. Reflections on metallic walls."
      },
      "subject": {
        "constraints": {
          "facial_identity": "Match reference image exactly 100%",
          "face_edits": "None allowed"
        },
        "expression": [
          "Cool/Neutral",
          "Looking at phone screen",
          "Obscured by phone",
          "Sassy tilt"
        ],
        "pose": {
          "body_position": "Standing casually, hip cocked to one side.",
          "action": "Holding phone up to mirror, maybe one hand in pocket or adjusting hair.",
          "details": "Full body or 3/4 shot."
        },
        "clothing": {
          "style": "Streetwear or Night-out chic",
          "top": "Leather jacket or oversized blazer",
          "bottom": "Baggy cargo pants or mini skirt with patterned tights",
          "shoes": "Chunky platform boots or sneakers"
        },
        "accessories": [
          "Phone case with stickers",
          "Over-ear headphones around neck",
          "Beanie or cap"
        ]
      },

        "setting": "Inside a metal elevator",
        "background": [
          "Reflective metal walls",

The scene is set indoors in a modern room with a glossy wooden laminate floor and a background of white curtains casting soft shadows, illuminated by warm soft indoor light providing even illumination that enhances the skin tone. The final output is an 8K photorealistic image captured in a mirror selfie aesthetic with soft neutral tones, high but natural sharpness, and an elegant, calm, feminine mood, framed full body centered in the 4:5 aspect ratio, using an eye-level reflection angle, with sharp focus on the face and soft room depth.

![四个超写实女性肖像提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765421915407_c7adsw_G7ipAOtaYAAGjx_.jpg)
![四个超写实女性肖像提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765421915325_yqtkal_G7ipASHbMAARzPK.jpg)
![四个超写实女性肖像提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765421915531_skmvey_G7ipASyaYAANPG3.jpg)
![四个超写实女性肖像提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765421916926_yq9zo1_G7ipAWQaIAAoy6j.jpg)

```
Prompt 1:
"A close-up, half-body mirror selfie of a young woman( match face) standing indoors. She is wearing a cozy, white, crew-neck sweater adorned with large, plush, red heart appliques scattered across the front and sleeves. She is also wearing light-wash blue denim jeans. Her hair is pulled up into a messy bun. She has a delicate gold necklace with a small pendant. The background is simple and bright, showing a neutral-toned wall and a doorway with a silver handle. Soft, natural lighting."

Prompt 2:
"Ultra-realistic high-detail indoor portrait of a beautiful woman - keep her real face, natural features, body proportions, and hair EXACTLY the same as the reference (no facial or body changes).
She is wearing a soft {argument name="dress color" default="lavender"} embroidered bodycon dress (updated wearing color), detailed stitching, elegant contours, and a refined luxury-fit silhouette.
Natural soft makeup with smooth skin texture and subtle highlights. Lighting: warm, soft indoor lighting, gentle shadows, natural glow on the face, smooth even complexion, premium portrait depth.
Background: subtle indoor blur (bokeh effect), clean aesthetic, minimal distraction, creamy depth-of-field.
Quality: sharp facial details, natural skin texture, smooth gradients, premium color grading, elegant portrait composition."

Prompt 3:
"Create a photorealistic image of a young woman(match face) sitting at a relaxed outdoor restaurant in {argument name="city" default="London"} on a cool {argument name="day of week" default="Wednesday"} morning in {argument name="month" default="March"} {argument name="year" default="2025"}. The sky is clear, the spring air is crisp, and the city feels calm as it wakes up. She is the focal point of the shot-wearing a light scarf, a black coat and a black turtle neck inside, gently stirring her coffee while gazing off to the side with a thoughtful expression. Everything behind her, from the waiter moving about to the soft morning traffic, should fall into a smooth blur, giving the picture the effortless, candid atmosphere of a moment casually snapped on a phone."

Prompt 4:
"A woman(match face from reference) is holding a cat gently with both hands, looking at it with a soft smile. Her expression is calm, tender, and affectionate. She has long, messy dark brown hair and is wearing a light brown ribbed long-sleeve shirt with buttons. She has small simple earrings, a delicate chain necklace, a thin silver ring on her left hand, and a small botanical tattoo on her right wrist.
The cat is light-colored with cream and beige fur. It sits securely in her arms, looking back at her with a calm, curious expression.
The scene takes place in an indoor room with a plain, neutral-colored wall. Warm sunlight comes through window blinds, casting soft striped shadows across both the woman and the cat.
The overall aesthetic is a soft, natural portrait with a warm, gentle, intimate vibe. The tones include warm beige, soft brown, and natural skin tones. The mood captures a peaceful moment between a human and her pet."

### 87. 自拍肖像的详细 JSON 提示

**Author**: [𝗦𝗮𝗻𝗶𝗮](https://x.com/saniaspeaks_)  **Date**: 2025-12-06  **Language**: en

> 这是一个为 Nano Banana Pro 设计的高度结构化的 JSON 提示，用于生成一张特写、平视的镜面自拍肖像。它详细指定了照片风格、光线（柔和温暖的室内光）、主体（姿势、表情、服装）、环境（卧室/更衣室）和美学（自然生活方式自拍，干净中性的调色板）的参数。

![自拍肖像的详细 JSON 提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765438496413_wra58g_G7gtZHybsAAQXBs.jpg)

```
{
  "image_generation": {
    "face": {
      "preserve_original": true,
      "reference_match": true
   },
    "photo_style": {
      "type": "mirror selfie portrait",
      "camera_angle": "close-up to medium shot, eye-level via mirror reflection",
      "lighting": "soft warm indoor lighting with low contrast",
      "mood": "calm, introspective, minimal",
      "texture": "natural skin texture, soft shadows, subtle grain",
      "focus": "sharp focus on subject and phone reflection, background softly blurred"
    },

    "subject": {
      "pose": "standing indoors holding a smartphone up for a mirror selfie, head slightly turned to the side",
      "expression": "neutral, thoughtful, relaxed",
      "hair": {
        "style": "long, straight to slightly wavy, loose",
        "color": "natural brown"
      },
      "clothing": {
        "type": "casual indoor wear",
        "details": "loose dark-colored t-shirt with minimal styling"
      },
      "accessories": {
        "phone": "smartphone visible in hand with camera interface reflected in mirror"
      }
    },

    "environment": {
      "setting": "bedroom or dressing room",
      "background": "mirror surface, clothing rack, drawers, softly lit interior space",
      "atmosphere": "quiet, personal, cozy indoor environment"
    },

    "aesthetic": {
      "style": "natural lifestyle selfie",
      "features": [
        "mirror reflection composition",
        "soft ambient indoor lighting",
        "minimalist fashion",
        "casual everyday setting",
        "clean neutral color palette"
      ]
    }
  }
}
```

### 88. 带面部保留的镜面自拍提示

**Author**: [毎日の活力⚡](https://x.com/_dailyboost)  **Date**: 2025-12-06  **Language**: en

> 一个高度详细的 JSON 提示，用于生成一位年轻女性在现代公寓中拍摄的镜面自拍，特别要求根据上传的图像 100% 保留面部特征，包括面部比例和自然的皮肤纹理。

```
{
  "image_generation": {
    "subject": {
"face": "same as uploaded image",
      "description": "Young woman taking a mirror selfie inside a modern living room.",
      "face_preservation": {
        "preserve_original": true,
        "accuracy_level": "100% identical to the reference image",
        "details": [
          "real facial proportions",
          "natural skin texture",
          "true eye shape and brows",
          "soft rosy lips",
          "light natural makeup"
        ]
      },

      "expression": "soft, slightly pouty expression with relaxed eyes",
      
      "hair": {
        "style": "long wavy hair styled in a half-up half-down look with soft volume",
        "color": "dark brown"
      },

      "pose": {
        "type": "mirror selfie",
        "description": "sitting sideways on a couch, upper body turned slightly toward mirror, one hand holding the phone while the other rests on her leg",
        "camera_angle": "eye-level, reflected in mirror"
      },

      "clothing": {
        "main_outfit": "pink and purple floral mini dress with long sheer sleeves",
        "fit": "form-fitting with ruched details",
        "accessories": [
          "gold hoop earrings",
          "delicate gold bracelet",
          "simple rings"
        ]
      },

      "hands": {
        "details": "holding green phone with floral-patterned case, nails neatly manicured"
      }
    },

    "environment": {
      "setting": "bright modern apartment interior",
      "elements": [
        "decorative frosted floral mirror pattern",
        "large living room area",
        "white sectional couch",
        "kitchen visible in background",
        "soft carpet, coffee table with decor items"
      ],
      "lighting": {
        "type": "soft natural daylight",
        "source": "large windows from the left side",
        "effect": "gentle, even illumination with natural skin glow"
      }
    },

    "composition": {
      "frame": "mid-shot, capturing upper body and part of seated pose",
      "style": "natural lifestyle photography",
      "focus": "sharp on subject's face and outfit, slightly softer background"
    },

    "camera": {
      "type": "iPhone mirror selfie",
      "aspect_ratio": "9:16 vertical",
      "quality": "realistic high-resolution smartphone capture"
    },

    "aesthetic": {
      "mood": "soft, feminine, calm",
      "color_palette": "pinks, purples, neutral beige and white",
      "details": [
        "subtle bokeh",
        "clean and modern interior atmosphere"
      ]
    }
  }
}
```

![低保真闭路电视监控画面图像](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769495326188_slg07g_G_kiPLRWEAE2CHc.jpg)

```
{
  "image_description": {
    "title": "Surveillance Feed: Defiant Subject in Retail Shop",
    "aspect_ratio": "4:5",
    "mood": "Raw, gritty, confrontational, authentic"
  },
  "visual_elements": {
    "subject": {
      "framing": "Centered from mid-torso upward",
      "pose": "Head tilted back looking up at camera, relaxed yet defiant posture",
      "action": "Hand raised with middle finger extended (silhouette, ghosted by motion)",
      "facial_features": "Largely obscured by blur, mouth open with tongue faintly visible",
      "apparel": "Dark oversized sunglasses reflecting ambient light"
    },
    "environment": {
      "location": "Cramped retail shop interior",
      "foreground": "Cluttered checkout counter, papers, white shopping bag with red rope handles",
      "background": "Densely packed shelves with small items, souvenirs, and figurines (abstracted by low resolution)"
    }
  },
  "technical_specifications": {

    "lens_distortion": "Subtle fisheye warping at frame edges",
    "lighting": "Harsh flat fluorescent, blown highlights, dull shadows",
    "color_grading": "Cool green-blue cast, uneven color reproduction, visible banding, reduced dynamic range"
  },

    "quality": "Intentionally degraded, low-fidelity",
    "artifacts": [
      "Strong motion blur",
      "Digital smearing",
      "Compression artifacts",
      "Heavy noise",
      "Scan lines"
    ],
    "sharpness": "Low perceived sharpness, distinct details stretched and indistinct"
  },
  "full_prompt_text": "A heavily distorted, low-fidelity surveillance-style image depicts the Subject standing behind a cramped retail checkout counter inside a cluttered shop, captured from a high-mounted camera angled steeply downward in a top-down CCTV perspective. The image quality is intentionally degraded, with strong motion blur, digital smearing, compression artifacts, heavy noise, scan lines, and subtle fisheye distortion warping the frame edges, making fine details indistinct and stretched. The Subject is centered from mid-torso upward, looking up toward the camera with the head tilted back; facial features are largely obscured by blur and artifacts, though dark oversized sunglasses dominate the face, reflecting ambient light, and the mouth appears open with the tongue faintly visible. One hand is raised toward the camera with the middle finger extended, clearly readable in silhouette but softened and ghosted by motion and low clarity, conveying a relaxed yet defiant posture. > 一个高度具体的提示，旨在生成一张不完美、原始、真实的抓拍照片，模仿夜晚匆忙用智能手机闪光灯拍摄的效果。它详细描述了场景（东京人行道）、拍摄对象的反应（转头、抬手挡住镜头、羞涩的微笑）以及技术缺陷（严重的运动模糊、刺眼的闪光灯、高噪点、不完美的构图）。负面提示内容广泛，明确拒绝了精致、电影感或理想化的美学效果。

![原始的、运动模糊的夜间智能手机闪光灯人像](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768319118515_4vfv69_G-dJbt2aUAAkbye.jpg)

```
Ultra-realistic candid smartphone photograph,
9:16 vertical.

Use the attached image only as a strong visual inspiration for general facial proportions and vibe,
while ensuring the generated subject remains fully original, non-identifiable, and not a face copy.

Scene
Nighttime on a quiet Tokyo city sidewalk beside a building with white ceramic tile walls.
The subject is walking past the camera, partially side-on, captured mid-step in a rushed, accidental moment.

Poses & Gestures (combined naturally)
The subject reacts instinctively to being photographed:
turning her head back mid-walk as if surprised,
raising one hand close to the lens to partially block the camera,
shy, restrained smile forming as she suppresses laughter,
body angled in half-profile while continuing to walk forward,
motion carries her slightly out of frame, imperfect framing.
Expressions are subtle and spontaneous — embarrassed, playful, fleeting — never posed.

Camera & Motion
Shot on a modern smartphone, handheld, rushed capture. Strong uncontrolled camera shake. Heavy directional motion blur across the raised hand, hair, and face. Facial features appear smeared and streaked by movement, faintly recognizable but distorted. Partial ghosting around the body. Imperfect framing, subject nearly leaving the frame.

Lighting
Flash-only lighting fired mid-motion. Harsh flash highlights on skin and hand. Deep surrounding darkness. Uneven exposure, blown highlights, hard shadows typical of hurried night phone photography.

Background
White ceramic tile wall stretches into streaked light bands due to motion blur. Street surroundings fade into darkness with minimal readable detail.

Mood
Candid, shy, slightly playful. Feels intrusive, raw, imperfect, and authentic — like a fleeting memory accidentally captured and never meant to be perfect.

Image Quality
Extremely noisy. Heavily blurred. Raw smartphone look. Not cinematic. Not editorial. Not polished.

Negative Prompt
anime, illustration, painting, stylized,
studio lighting, beauty lighting, soft portrait,
sharp focus, clean face, perfect anatomy, smooth skin,
fashion editorial, posed portrait, cinematic grading, film still,
tripod shot, professional photography,
identity match, face copy, real person replication.

– no anime, illustration, cartoon, or doll-like features
– no beauty filters, no airbrushed skin
– no face reshaping or eye enlargement
– no exaggerated body curves
– no extra or missing fingers
– no distorted arms, shoulders, or neck
– no studio or cinematic lighting
– no fashion posing
```

### 112. 意大利面化故障特效（洛基灵感）

**Author**: [BeautyVerse](https://x.com/BeautyVerse_Lab)  **Date**: 2025-12-14  **Language**: en

> 一个多层提示，旨在重现《洛基》电视剧中出现的“意大利面化”或瓦解效果。它使用四个不同的指令层，以确保背景稳定、主体边缘剧烈地解体成不发光的丝带、仅集中在边缘的模拟故障叠加，以及主体身后幽灵般的运动模糊残影。

![意大利面化故障特效（洛基灵感）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765991248279_gjghqt_G8HAxWObYAEmmL0.jpg)
![意大利面化故障特效（洛基灵感）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765991248575_bycdfc_G8HAxWkbgAAqc9h.jpg)

```
(Photorealistic:1.3), raw photograph, cinematic lighting, sharp focus on the subject’s face and eyes, crisp skin texture.
LAYER 1: BACKGROUND STABILITY (CRITICAL):

The entire background environment from the input image remains completely STATIC, FROZEN, CLEAN, and UNCHANGED — no noise, no scanlines, no distortions, no glitches in the background.
LAYER 2: FOREGROUND SUBJECT EDGE-CHAOS:

The main subject’s core (face/torso) stays clear and undistorted, BUT the outer silhouette boundaries are unraveling violently into long ribbons of (non-glowing physical matter:1.3), showing stretched fabric/leather/latex-like material with realistic strand separation and tearing flow (“Spaghettification”), no gore.
LAYER 3: ANALOG GLITCH OVERLAY (EDGE-ONLY):

Heavy VHS static, scan lines, color bleed, and screen tearing noise are CONCENTRATED EXCLUSIVELY ON THE UNRAVELING EDGES of the main subject, like an edge mask. No full-frame VHS overlay; the core and background remain clean.
LAYER 4: GHOSTLY AFTERIMAGES (BEHIND SUBJECT):

Directly BEHIND the unraveling main subject, visible through the gaps, there are TWO translucent, ghostly motion-blur AFTERIMAGES. They are violently twisted into agonizing, struggling postures, dragged by temporal distortion. They remain behind the subject, partially occluded, not separate characters.

Negative prompt (optional but recommended):

full-frame glitch, background distortion, extra people, duplicate main subject, neon glow, energy beams, particles, blood, gore, exposed organs, messy face, blurry eyes, deformed hands
```

[[Motion Blur]] [[Glitch Art]]

**Author**: [Mr Das](https://x.com/MrDasOnX)  **Date**: 2026-03-15  **Language**: en

> 一个高度详细的 JSON 提示，用于让 Nano Banana 2 生成一张超逼真的、自然的智能手机自拍照，拍摄地点是白天现代汽车的内部。该提示要求使用上传的照片作为精确的面部参考，并指定精确的相机模拟（iPhone 前置摄像头）、自然日光、可见的皮肤纹理和放松的姿势，同时使用大量的负面提示来防止人工编辑。

```
{
  "aspect_ratio": "9:16",
  "prompt": "A realistic front-facing smartphone selfie of the same woman (use uploaded photo as exact face reference, preserve every facial feature, skin detail and expression without alteration or beautification) taken inside a modern car during daytime. Framed from upper chest to top of head, she's sitting in the driver's seat, holding a dark gray iPhone (visible triple-camera module) in her right hand extended at classic selfie distance (~arm's length), looking directly into the phone screen with a relaxed, subtle closed-mouth smile and natural eye contact. Shot simulation: smartphone front camera ~24-28mm equivalent, natural wide-angle perspective with very mild edge distortion typical of phone selfies, eye-level framing. Bright natural daylight streaming through windshield and side windows (mid-morning to early afternoon, clear weather), creating soft even illumination on face with gentle highlights on cheekbones/nose/forehead, subtle catchlights in eyes, realistic soft shadows under chin and from dashboard below. Preserve authentic skin: visible pores, natural texture, light imperfections, subtle oil sheen if present, no smoothing or filters. Medium-length dark brown hair with soft loose waves, slightly tousled from driving, a few strands across forehead. Wearing casual everyday outfit: fitted white cotton t-shirt or simple crew-neck tee, light denim jacket or open cardigan, small gold necklace and stud earrings. Delicate fine-line tattoo visible on inner right forearm if in reference.
